"For quite some time I struggled with eating disorders because I was constantly trying to keep my weight really low, to appear more, like those women are covers," she says.;“在很长一段时间里，我一直在与饮食失调作斗争，因为我一直在努力保持我的体重非常低，看起来更多，就像那些女人是被覆盖物一样，”她说。
"For quite some time I struggled with eating disorders because I was constantly trying to keep my weight really low, to appear more, like those women are on those covers," she says.;“在很长一段时间里，我一直在与饮食失调作斗争，因为我一直在努力保持体重非常低，看起来更多，就像那些女人戴着那些被子一样，”她说。
覆盖物

"For quite some time I struggled with eating disorders because I was constantly trying to keep my weight really low, to appear more, like those women are covers," she says.;“在很长一段时间里，我一直在与饮食失调作斗争，因为我一直在努力保持我的体重非常低，看起来更多，就像那些女人是被覆盖物一样，”她说。
